The formatter parser (SubstitutionFormatParser) tries command parsers in this order:\n   - Built-in command parsers (from BuiltInCommandParsersBase)\n   - User-provided command parsers\n   - Context-independent formatters (StreamInfoFormatterBase)\n\n2.
